<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
var sPageURL = window.location.search.substring(1);
var sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&');
var finalString = '';
for (var i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++)
{
var sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');
if (sParameterName[0].indexOf("utm_")!=-1 || sParameterName[0].indexOf("gclid")!=-1)
{
if(finalString != ''){
finalString = finalString + '&';
}
finalString = finalString + encodeURIComponent(sParameterName[0]) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(sParameterName[1]);
}
}
if(finalString != ''){
$("#affiliateTrackingCode").html("<iframe src='http://tracker.homeshop18.com/scripts/track.php?" + finalString + "' scrolling='no' width='1' height='1' marginheight='0' marginwidth='0' frameborder='0'></iframe>");
}
});
</script>
